+___    ______ ____    _____ _____  ____ __ ______    ______ _________
0                                   6660              ¿þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþÜ
                                    6661              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6662              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6663              Ÿ  SETWDICT -- SET WDICTIONARY Command.  (Priv'd.)                    Ÿ
                                    6664              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6665              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6666              Ÿ   WE MAKE A DICTIONARY                                              Ÿ
                                    6667              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6668              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6669              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6670              Ÿ  Make a compressed dictionary and a index into it.                  Ÿ
                                    6671              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6672              Ÿ  We read in an alphabetized list of words and create an in core     Ÿ
                                    6673              Ÿ  dictionary.  The dictionary is compressed using a simple scheeme.  Ÿ
                                    6674              Ÿ  The words in the input file are in alphabetical order.  The        Ÿ
                                    6675              Ÿ  letters at the start of each word that are in common with the      Ÿ
                                    6676              Ÿ  previous word are changed to blanks.  These blanks are then        Ÿ
                                    6677              Ÿ  compressed using the wylbur edit format compression scheem.        Ÿ
                                    6678              Ÿ  Additionally, each word is preceeded by a blank that acts as       Ÿ
                                    6679              Ÿ  a word separator.  The leading blank is compressed as are the      Ÿ
                                    6680              Ÿ  other blanks in wylbur edit format fashion.  See example  !!!      Ÿ
                                    6681              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6682              Ÿ  Example:                                                           Ÿ
                                    6683              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6684              Ÿ     list:           compressed list:       sample output:           Ÿ
                                    6685              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6686              Ÿ       bat              bat                   x'13',c'bat'           Ÿ
                                    6687              Ÿ       batting             ting               x'44',c'ting'          Ÿ
                                    6688              Ÿ       battle               le                x'42',c'le'            Ÿ
                                    6689              Ÿ       butler            utler                x'25',c'utler'         Ÿ
                                    6690              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6691              Ÿ  Can you dig it !                                                   Ÿ
                                    6692              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6693              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6694              Ÿ  In addition to the dictionary, a 8192 entry index into the         Ÿ
                                    6695              Ÿ  dictionary is built.  The top (most used) two hundred words        Ÿ
                                    6696              Ÿ  are forced to be at the start of index entries.  this is a         Ÿ
                                    6697              Ÿ  random search optimization.  It is estimated that the 100 top      Ÿ
                                    6698              Ÿ  words are used about 50% of the time. hot city.                    Ÿ
                                    6699              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6700              Ÿ  Finally, we getmain enough core for a 120,000 word dictionary.     Ÿ
                                    6701              Ÿ  (appox 4 bytes per word entry). We freemain whatever core is       Ÿ
                                    6702              Ÿ  left over.  We set a use count byte on the dictionaries, so that   Ÿ
                                    6703              Ÿ  we may build and switch while wylbur is running.                   Ÿ
                                    6704              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6705              Ÿ***                                                                  Ÿ
                                                      ¾þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþ»

                                   14033              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14034              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14035              Ÿ    GUESSWD - GUESS CORRECT SPELLING, (IE, FIND SIMILAR WORDS)       Ÿ
                                   14036              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14037              Ÿ       INPUTS:  R1,R0 - WORD LOCATION, LENGTH                        Ÿ
                                   14038              Ÿ                R15   - 0, OR RETURN AREA FOR GUESS WORDS.           Ÿ
                                   14039              Ÿ                        AREA SIZE IS ASSUMED TO BE 128 BYTES.        Ÿ
                                   14040              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14041              Ÿ       OUTPUTS: IF R15=0, SIMILAR WORDS ARE LISTED TO TERMINAL.      Ÿ
                                   14042              Ÿ                IF R15=RETURN AREA, WORDS ARE RETURNED IN AREA       Ÿ
                                   14043              Ÿ                EACH WORD IS 1 BYTE LENGTH FOLLOWED BY WORD, LIST    Ÿ
                                   14044              Ÿ                IS TERMINATED BY A ZERO LENGTH.                      Ÿ
                                   14045              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14046              Ÿ       RETURN CODES:                                                 Ÿ
                                   14047              Ÿ                R15=0,  RETURN AREA CONTAINS GUESSES                 Ÿ
                                   14048              Ÿ                R15=4,  WORD IS SPELLED CORRECTLY                    Ÿ
                                   14049              Ÿ                R15=8,  NO (GUESSES) SIMILAR WORDS FOUND             Ÿ
                                   14050              Ÿ                R15=12, GUESSES OVERFLOW 128 BYTE AREA               Ÿ
                                   14051              Ÿ                R16=16, NO SPELLING DICTIONARY AVAILABLE             Ÿ
                                   14052              Ÿ                R15=20, INVALID GUESS QUERY, ('*'1 OR '?'1)          Ÿ
                                   14053              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14054              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14055              Ÿ       THERE ARE THREE MODES OF OPERATION,                           Ÿ
                                   14056              Ÿ          IF '*' IN WORD, USE UNLIMITED SUBSTITUTION FOR '*'         Ÿ
                                   14057              Ÿ          IF '?' IN WORD, USE 1-1 LETTER SUBSTITUTIOTION FOR '?'     Ÿ
                                   14058              Ÿ          IF PLAIN WORD, IF CORRECT WE SAY SO, IF NOT CORRECT        Ÿ
                                   14059              Ÿ               WE GUESS CORRECT (IE. LIST SIMILAR) WORDS             Ÿ

0                                  18758              ¿þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþÜ
                                   18759              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   18760              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   18761              Ÿ       SCANTEXT - SCAN WORDS FORM INPUT TEXT,,,                      Ÿ
                                   18762              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   18763              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   18764              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   18765              Ÿ       ON ENTRY:                                                     Ÿ
                                   18766              Ÿ             R1 - SCAN PARAMETER BLOCK.                              Ÿ
                                   18767              Ÿ                     SCPTR,SCEND: START AND END OF STRING TO         Ÿ
                                   18768              Ÿ                     SCAN, MUST BE INITIALIZED IN PARM BLOCK         Ÿ
                                   18769              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   18770              Ÿ       ON EXIT:                                                      Ÿ
                                   18771              Ÿ             SCAN PARAMETER BLOCK FIELD UPDATED.                     Ÿ
                                   18772              Ÿ             R15 - CC, R15=0 WORD SCANNED, R15=NZ NULL SCAN          Ÿ
                                   18773              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   18774              Ÿ  NOTE, WE SCAN WORDS OF UP TO 64 CHARACTERS.  THIS ROUTINE IS       Ÿ
                                   18775              Ÿ  MOSTLY BASED ON THE TRT INSTRUCTION.  ACCEPTABLE CHARACTERS        Ÿ
                                   18776              Ÿ  IN WORDS ARE BASED ON TRT TABLES.  A PERIOD ('.'), FOR EXAMPLE,    Ÿ
                                   18777              Ÿ  IS OK IN THE MIDDLE OF A NAME, (IE. WYL.GG.USR.DSN) BUT NOT AT     Ÿ
                                   18778              Ÿ  THE BEGINING OR END OF A WORD.  WE USE 4 TRT TABLES:               Ÿ
                                   18779              Ÿ       1. ALPHATBL - SCAN FOR ALPHABETIC CHARACTERS.                 Ÿ
                                   18780              Ÿ       2. SEPTBL   - TABLE OF CHARACTERS USED AS SEPARATORS          Ÿ
                                   18781              Ÿ       3. STARTTBL - VALID STARTING CHARACTERS                       Ÿ
                                   18782              Ÿ       4. ENDTBL   - INVALID ENDING CHARACTERS                       Ÿ
                                   18783              Ÿ  IN SHORT, WE SCAN UNTIL A ALPHA. THEN WE BACK UP OVER VALID        Ÿ
                                   18784              Ÿ  STARTING CHARACTERS THAT MAY HAVE BEEN SKIPPED. THUS WE FIND       Ÿ
                                   18785              Ÿ  THE START OF WORD.  FOR THE END OF WORD, WE SCAN OVER WORD         Ÿ
                                   18786              Ÿ  LOOKING FOR END.  WE FIND THE END WHEN WE HIT A SEPARATOR.         Ÿ
                                   18787              Ÿ  THEN WE BACK UP OVER INVALID ENDING CHARACTERS.  THUS WE FIND      Ÿ
                                   18788              Ÿ  THE END OF THE WORD.                                               Ÿ
                                   18789              Ÿ       IN OTHER WORDS, WE DO A SCAN THAT IS A BIT COMPLICATED IN     Ÿ
                                   18790              Ÿ  THAT THERE ARE THREE PLACES IN WHICH WE CHECK A CHARACTERS         Ÿ
                                   18791              Ÿ  VALIDITY WITHIN A WORD, DEPENDING ON WHETHER THE CHARACTER IS AT   Ÿ
                                   18792              Ÿ  THE START, MIDDLE OR END OF THE WORD.  SEE THE CODE AND TRT        Ÿ
                                   18793              Ÿ  TABLES FOR PARTICULARS.                                            Ÿ
                                   18794              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   18795              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                                      ¾þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþ»
